[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhigh‐severity memory safety issue.[0m                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The invalid write occurs in `__asan_memcpy` called by `tvb_memcpy`  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     at packet-tvbuff.[0m[1;92mc:945[0m[39m and then in `tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz`  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvbuff.[0m[1;92mc:4047[0m[39m and [0m[1;36m4073[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The next frame in the stack is `telnet_add_text` at packet-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:2211[0m[39m,  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     which is invoked by `dissect_telnet` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:2337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                 [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     earlier in the `dissect_telnet` logic.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2179[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2180[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:635[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m643[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m635[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;92m636:d[0m[1;35missect_linemode_subopt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info *pinfo, const char *optname _U_, tvbuff_t [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*tvb _U_, int offset _U_,[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m637[0m[39m:                    int len _U_, proto_tree *tree _U_, proto_item *item _U_[0m[1;39m)[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m638[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m639[0m[39m:  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set [0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m640[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m641[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m642[0m[39m:  return;[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m643[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/dissectors/packet-telnet.[0m[1;92mc:2190[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m2214[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2190[0m[39m:static void[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2191[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mtelnet_add_text[0m[1;39m([0m[39mproto_tree *tree, tvbuff_t *tvb, int offset, int len[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2192[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2193[0m[39m:  int      next_offset;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2194[0m[39m:  int      linelen;[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2195[0m[39m:  uint8_t  c;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2196[0m[39m:  bool last_char_was_cr;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2197[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2198[0m[39m:  while [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlen != [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m && [0m[1;35mtvb_offset_exists[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2199[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m*[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2200[0m[39m:     * Find the end of the line.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2201[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2202[0m[39m:    linelen = [0m[1;35mtvb_find_line_end[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, len, &next_offset, false[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2203[0m[39m:    len -= next_offset - offset;        [0m[35m/[0m[39m* subtract out the line's characters [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m*[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2204[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2205[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Telnet RFC [0m[1;36m1184[0m[39m allows for specifying window size via columns and [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheight.[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2206[0m[39m:       If this subopt is set then a method for storing the data in a given [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwindow[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2207[0m[39m:       is necessary.[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2208[0m[39m:    *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2209[0m[39m:   if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2210[0m[39m:    int start_offset = hf_telnet_width * hf_telnet_line;[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2211[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mtvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset, [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinelen < hf_telnet_width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlinelen : hf_telnet_width, hf_naws_data + start_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2212[0m[39m:    hf_telnet_line = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_line + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m % hf_telnet_height;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2213[0m[39m:  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2214[0m[39m:[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Identify and confirm the root cause  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The NAWS sub-option handler [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_naws_subopt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allocates a buffer [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`hf_naws_data` and sets the flag `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set`.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A separate sub-option handler [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_linemode_subopt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m frees that same [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer via `[0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when any LINEMODE sub-option is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseen, but leaves the flag `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set` still set.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Later, in `telnet_add_text`, the code checks only `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mnot the pointer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and unconditionally writes into `hf_naws_data`, which may have [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeen freed—triggering the heap-use-after-free.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preserve existing functionality  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to allocate and use the NAWS buffer in `dissect_naws_subopt` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand allow `telnet_add_text` to copy telnet text into it when NAWS is enabled.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - We must continue to support LINEMODE and other sub-options without breaking [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtheir parsing.  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch strategy—two complementary changes in packet-telnet.c  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   a[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Prevent stale-flag use-after-free in `dissect_linemode_subopt`  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Either remove the freeing of the NAWS buffer here [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpreferred, since memory [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis pool‐managed and will be reclaimed at end of packet lifecycle[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, or if one wishes[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto keep the free, immediately clear both the flag and the pointer to avoid [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msubsequent misuse.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Example patch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mclear state after free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:  [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        static void[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mdissect_linemode_subopt[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info *pinfo, const char *optname _U_,[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                               tvbuff_t *tvb _U_, int offset _U_, int len _U_,[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                               proto_tree *tree _U_, proto_item *item _U_[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            [0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo->pool, hf_naws_data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            hf_naws_data = NULL;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Or simply remove the `[0m[1;35mwmem_free[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` call and reset the flag & pointer:  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        static void[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mdissect_linemode_subopt[0m[1;39m([0m[39m…[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[35m/[0m[39m* LINEMODE sub-option does not own the NAWS buffer; reset state only *[0m[35m/[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m            hf_naws_data = NULL;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          return;[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   b[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m Harden `telnet_add_text` against a NULL or freed `hf_naws_data`  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Strengthen the guard so it checks both the flag and the pointer before [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcopying:  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```c[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_naws_subopt_set && hf_naws_data != NULL[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          int start_offset = hf_telnet_width * hf_telnet_line;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mtvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtvb, offset,[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                       [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlinelen < hf_telnet_width[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ? linelen : [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhf_telnet_width,[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                       hf_naws_data + start_offset[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          hf_telnet_line = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mhf_telnet_line + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m % hf_telnet_height;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - This ensures that even if the flag somehow remains set, no write occurs [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minto a NULL or freed buffer.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removing or guarding the free in `dissect_linemode_subopt` prevents the [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpremature deallocation of the NAWS buffer while still allowing normal pool‐scoped [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory management to reclaim the buffer at the end of packet processing.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Clearing `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set` and `hf_naws_data` immediately upon free [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mguarantees that later calls to `telnet_add_text` will not believe a valid buffer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mremains.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Strengthening the `telnet_add_text` guard adds a second line of defense, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring that even if future changes forget to clear the flag, no UAF will occur.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These changes do not affect external/internal tests or fuzz harness code, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpreserve existing Telnet parsing logic, and do not touch non‐Telnet or harness [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode.[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigations  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The only removed operation is freeing the NAWS buffer inside [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_linemode_subopt`. Since the buffer is allocated from a wmem [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpool[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallocator, it will be automatically reclaimed when the packet‐scan memory pool is [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdestroyed. There is no lasting memory leak.  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If for some reason the buffer must be freed earlier, the added pointer‐null [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcheck in `telnet_add_text` prevents misuse but skips copying NAWS data if the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer was freed. This is acceptable because freeing signals end of NAWS use.  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other protocol features or suboptions are touched, and the TELNET harness [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mfuzzer entry point[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m remains unchanged.  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Tests covering Telnet NAWS or LINEMODE functionality should continue to pass. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. References to similar code  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other dissectors using wmem pools [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., X Display, SSH[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m rely on pool‐scoped [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlifetime without explicit frees inside sub-option handlers. They do not free [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mper‐suboption and thus avoid stale‐flag UAFs.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This fix aligns Telnet’s handling with those patterns.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
